Copilot 2026/04/19 15:25

数据结构已清楚：
- 大鼠 MCAO 卒中模型，4 组（Young/Aged × sham/MCAO）
- 基因符号为大鼠格式（Fam111a → 人类 FAM111A）
- 需要 rat→human 转换才能对接疾病/中药靶点数据库

现在创建完整的网络药理学分析脚本：

DEG ∩ 疾病: %d\\n\", length(intersect(deg_set, disease_set))))\n  cat(sprintf(\"    DEG ∩ 中药: %d\\n\", length(intersect(deg_set, herb_set))))\n  cat(sprintf(\"    疾病 ∩ 中药: %d\\n\", length(intersect(disease_set, herb_set))))\n}\n\n# 选择用于后续分析的基因集\nif (length(intersection_3way) >= 5) {\n  target_genes <- intersection_3way\n  cat(\"  → 使用三者交集进行后续分析\\n\")\n} else if (length(intersection_3way) >= 1) {\n  # 三者交集不足 5 个 → 加入 DEG∩疾病 和 DEG∩中药 的并集\n  target_genes <- union(\n    intersection_3way,\n    intersect(deg_set, union(disease_set, herb_set))\n  )\n  cat(sprintf(\"  → 三者交集不足, 扩大为 DEG ∩ (疾病 ∪ 中药): %d 个基因\\n\", length(target_genes)))\n} else {\n  target_genes <- intersect(deg_set, union(disease_set, herb_set))\n  cat(sprintf(\"  → 三者交集为空, 使用 DEG ∩ (疾病 ∪ 中药): %d 个基因\\n\", length(target_genes)))\n}\n\nif (length(target_genes) < 2) {\n  stop(\"可用基因不足 2 个。请检查疾病基因和中药靶点数据是否完整。\")\n}\n\nwrite.csv(\n  data.frame(gene_symbol = target_genes),\n element_text(hjust = 0.5, face = \"bold\"))\n\nggsave(file.path(out_dir, \"04_venn_diagram.pdf\"), p_venn, width = 8, height = 7)\ncat(\"  已保存: 04_venn_diagram.pdf\\n\")\n\n\n# ╔════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════╗\n# ║  Step 5: STRING PPI 网络                                                  ║\n# ╚════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════╝\n\ncat(\"\\n══ Step 5: PPI 网络 (STRING) ══\\n\")\n\n# --- 方法 A: STRING REST API (更稳定) ---\nbuild_ppi_from_rest <- function(genes, species = 9606, score_threshold = 400) {\n  # 分批查询 (STRING 限制每次 2000 个基因)\n  batch_size <- 500\n  all_interactions <- list()\n\n  for (i in seq(1, length(genes), by = batch_size)) {\n    batch <- genes[i:min(i + batch_size - 1, length(genes))]\n    url   <- \"https://string-db.org/api/json/network\"\n    res   <- tryCatch(\n      GET(url, query = list(\n        identifiers    = paste(batch, collapse = \"\\r\"),\n        species        = species,\n        required_score = score_threshold,\n        caller_identity = \"network_pharmacology_R\"\n      ), timeout(120)),\n      error = function(e) NULL\n    )\n\n    if (!is.null(res) && status_code(res) == 200) {\n      data <- fromJSON(content(res, \"text\", encoding = \"UTF-8\"))\n      if (is.data.frame(data) && nrow(data) > 0) {\n        all_interactions[[length(all_interactions) + 1]] <- data\n      }\n    }\n    Sys.sleep(1)  # 礼貌延迟\n  }\n\n  if (length(all_interactions) > 0) {\n    df <- bind_rows(all_interactions)\n    df <- df %>%\n      select(preferredName_A, preferredName_B, score) %>%\n      rename(gene1 = preferredName_A, gene2 = preferredName_B, combined_score = score) %>%\n      distinct()\n    return(df)\n  }\n  return(NULL)\n}\n\n# --- 方法 B: STRINGdb R 包 ---\nbuild_ppi_from_pkg <- function(genes, species = 9606, score_threshold = 400) {\n  tryCatch({\n    sdb    <- STRINGdb$new(version = \"12.0\", species = species,\n                           score_threshold = score_threshold, network_type = \"full\")\n    gene_df <- data.frame(gene = genes, stringsAsFactors = FALSE)\n    mapped  <- sdb$map(gene_df, \"gene\", removeUnmappedRows = TRUE)\n\n    if (nrow(mapped) < 2) return(NULL)\n\n    interactions <- sdb$get_interactions(mapped$STRING_id)\n    if (nrow(interactions) == 0) return(NULL)\n\n    id2gene <- setNames(mapped$gene, mapped$STRING_id)\n    interactions %>%\n      mutate(gene1 = id2gene[from], gene2 = id2gene[to]) %>%\n      filter(!is.na(gene1), !is.na(gene2)) %>%\n      select(gene1, gene2, combined_score)\n  }, error = function(e) {\n    message(\"    STRINGdb R 包查询失败: \", conditionMessage(e))\n    NULL\n  })\n}\n\n# 先尝试 REST API, 失败则用 R 包\ncat(\"  正在查询 STRING (REST API)...\\n\")\nppi_df <- build_ppi_from_rest(target_genes)\n\nif (is.null(ppi_df) || nrow(ppi_df) == 0) {\n  cat(\"  REST API 无结果, 尝试 STRINGdb R 包...\\n\")\n  ppi_df <- build_ppi_from_pkg(target_genes)\n}\n\nif (is.null(ppi_df) || nrow(ppi_df) == 0) {\n  cat(\"  !! STRING 未返回互作数据。可能原因:\\n\")\n  cat(\"     1. 网络连接问题\\n\")\n  cat(\"     2. 交集基因在 STRING 中无互作\\n\")\n  cat(\"  → 请手动到 https://string-db.org/ 输入基因列表查询,\\n\")\n  cat(\"    导出 TSV 保存为:\", file.path(out_dir, \"05_PPI_interactions.csv\"), \"\\n\")\n  cat(\"    列名: gene1, gene2, combined_score\\n\")\n\n  # 尝试读取用户手动上传的文件\n  manual_ppi <- file.path(out_dir, \"05_PPI_interactions.csv\")\n  if (file.exists(manual_ppi)) {\n    ppi_df <- read.csv(manual_ppi, stringsAsFactors = FALSE)\n    cat(\"  从手动文件读取 PPI 数据\\n\")\n  } else {\n    stop(\"无法获取 PPI 数据, 请检查网络或手动下载\")\n  }\n}\n\ncat(sprintf(\"  PPI 互作边数: %d\\n\", nrow(ppi_df)))\n\n# 保存 PPI (可导入 Cytoscape)\nwrite.csv(ppi_df, file.path(out_dir, \"05_PPI_interactions.csv\"), row.names = FALSE)\n\n# 导出 Cytoscape SIF 格式\nwrite.table(\n  ppi_df[, c(\"gene1\", \"gene2\")],\n  file.path(out_dir, \"05_PPI_for_cytoscape.sif\"),\n  sep = \"\\t\", row.names = FALSE, col.names = FALSE, quote = FALSE\n)\n\n# --- 用 igraph 构建网络 ---\ng <- graph_from_data_frame(ppi_df[, c(\"gene1\", \"gene2\")], directed = FALSE)\ng <- simplify(g)\n\n# 删除孤立节点\niso <- which(degree(g) == 0)\nif (length(iso) > 0) g <- delete_vertices(g, iso)\n\nV(g)$degree <- degree(g)\n\ncat(sprintf(\"  PPI 网络: %d 节点, %d 边\\n\", vcount(g), ecount(g)))\n\n# --- PPI 网络可视化 ---\npdf(file.path(out_dir, \"05_PPI_network_plot.pdf\"), width = 14, height = 14)\nset.seed(42)\nn_colors   <- max(V(g)$degree, na.rm = TRUE)\npal        <- colorRampPalette(c(\"#5DADE2\", \"#F4D03F\", \"#E74C3C\"))(n_colors + 1)\nV(g)$color <- pal[V(g)$degree + 1]\nV(g)$size  <- rescale(V(g)$degree, to = c(5, 22))\nV(g)$label.cex <- rescale(V(g)$degree, to = c(0.5, 1.3))\nV(g)$frame.color <- NA\n\nplot(g,\n     layout          = layout_with_fr(g),\n     vertex.label.color = \"grey10\",\n     edge.color      = adjustcolor(\"grey60\", alpha.f = 0.5),\n     edge.width      = 0.8,\n     main            = paste0(\"PPI Network (\", vcount(g), \" nodes, \", ecount(g), \" edges)\"))\ndev.off()\ncat(\"  已保存: 05_PPI_network_plot.pdf\\n\")\n\n\n# ╔════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════╗\n# ║  Step 6: GO / KEGG 富集分析                                               ║\n# ╚════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════╝\n\ncat(\"\\n══ Step 6: GO / KEGG 富集分析 ══\\n\")\n\n# 基因 Symbol → Entrez ID\ngene_ids <- bitr(target_genes, fromType = \"SYMBOL\", toType = \"ENTREZID\",\n                 OrgDb = org.Hs.eg.db)\ncat(sprintf(\"  SYMBOL → ENTREZ 转换: %d / %d\\n\", nrow(gene_ids), length(target_genes)))\n\nentrez_list <- unique(gene_ids$ENTREZID)\n\n# --- GO 富集 ---\nego_bp <- enrichGO(gene = entrez_list, OrgDb = org.Hs.eg.db, ont = \"BP\",\n                   pAdjustMethod = \"BH\", pvalueCutoff = 0.05, qvalueCutoff = 0.2,\n                   readable = TRUE)\nego_cc <- enrichGO(gene = entrez_list, OrgDb = org.Hs.eg.db, ont = \"CC\",\n                   pAdjustMethod = \"BH\", pvalueCutoff = 0.05, qvalueCutoff = 0.2,\n                   readable = TRUE)\nego_mf <- enrichGO(gene = entrez_list, OrgDb = org.Hs.eg.db, ont = \"MF\",\n                   pAdjustMethod = \"BH\", pvalueCutoff = 0.05, qvalueCutoff = 0.2,\n                   readable = TRUE)\n\n# --- KEGG 富集 ---\nekegg <- enrichKEGG(gene = entrez_list, organism = \"hsa\",\n                    pvalueCutoff = 0.05, qvalueCutoff = 0.2)\n\n# --- 保存 CSV ---\ngo_kegg_results <- list(\n  GO_BP = ego_bp, GO_CC = ego_cc, GO_MF = ego_mf, KEGG = ekegg\n)\nfor (nm in names(go_kegg_results)) {\n  obj <- go_kegg_results[[nm]]\n  if (!is.null(obj) && nrow(as.data.frame(obj)) > 0) {\n    write.csv(as.data.frame(obj), file.path(out_dir, paste0(\"06_\", nm, \".csv\")), row.names = FALSE)\n    cat(sprintf(\"  %s: %d 条显著通路\\n\", nm, nrow(as.data.frame(obj))))\n  } else {\n    cat(sprintf(\"  %s: 无显著结果\\n\", nm))\n  }\n}\n\n# --- 可视化 ---\n# GO BP dotplot\nif (!is.null(ego_bp) && nrow(as.data.frame(ego_bp)) > 0) {\n  p1 <- dotplot(ego_bp, showCategory = 20, title = \"GO: Biological Process\") +\n    theme(axis.text.y = element_text(size = 8))\n  ggsave(file.path(out_dir, \"06_GO_BP_dotplot.pdf\"), p1, width = 10, height = 9)\n\n  p1b <- barplot(ego_bp, showCategory = 15, title = \"GO: Biological Process\")\n  ggsave(file.path(out_dir, \"06_GO_BP_barplot.pdf\"), p1b, width = 10, height = 8)\n}\n\n# GO CC dotplot\nif (!is.null(ego_cc) && nrow(as.data.frame(ego_cc)) > 0) {\n  p2 <- dotplot(ego_cc, showCategory = 15, title = \"GO: Cellular Component\") +\n    theme(axis.text.y = element_text(size = 8))\n  ggsave(file.path(out_dir, \"06_GO_CC_dotplot.pdf\"), p2, width = 10, height = 8)\n}\n\n# GO MF dotplot\nif (!is.null(ego_mf) && nrow(as.data.frame(ego_mf)) > 0) {\n  p3 <- dotplot(ego_mf, showCategory = 15, title = \"GO: Molecular Function\") +\n    theme(axis.text.y = element_text(size = 8))\n  ggsave(file.path(out_dir, \"06_GO_MF_dotplot.pdf\"), p3, width = 10, height = 8)\n}\n\n# KEGG dotplot\nif (!is.null(ekegg) && nrow(as.data.frame(ekegg)) > 0) {\n  p4 <- dotplot(ekegg, showCategory = 20, title = \"KEGG Pathway Enrichment\") +\n    theme(axis.text.y = element_text(size = 8))\n  ggsave(file.path(out_dir, \"06_KEGG_dotplot.pdf\"), p4, width = 10, height = 9)\n\n  p4b <- barplot(ekegg, showCategory = 15, title = \"KEGG Pathway Enrichment\")\n  ggsave(file.path(out_dir, \"06_KEGG_barplot.pdf\"), p4b, width = 10, height = 8)\n}\n\n# --- GO 三合一柱状图 (BP + CC + MF Top5) ---\ncombine_go_top <- function(bp, cc, mf, top_n = 5) {\n  dfs <- list()\n  if (!is.null(bp) && nrow(as.data.frame(bp)) > 0)\n    dfs[[\"BP\"]] <- as.data.frame(bp) %>% head(top_n) %>% mutate(Category = \"BP\")\n  if (!is.null(cc) && nrow(as.data.frame(cc)) > 0)\n    dfs[[\"CC\"]] <- as.data.frame(cc) %>% head(top_n) %>% mutate(Category = \"CC\")\n  if (!is.null(mf) && nrow(as.data.frame(mf)) > 0)\n    dfs[[\"MF\"]] <- as.data.frame(mf) %>% head(top_n) %>% mutate(Category = \"MF\")\n\n  if (length(dfs) == 0) return(NULL)\n  bind_rows(dfs) %>% select(Category, Description, Count, p.adjust)\n}\n\ngo_combined <- combine_go_top(ego_bp, ego_cc, ego_mf, top_n = 8)\nif (!is.null(go_combined) && nrow(go_combined) > 0) {\n  go_combined$Description <- factor(go_combined$Description,\n                                    levels = rev(go_combined$Description))\n  p_go3 <- ggplot(go_combined, aes(Count, Description, fill = Category)) +\n    geom_col(width = 0.7) +\n    scale_fill_manual(values = c(BP = \"#E74C3C\", CC = \"#27AE60\", MF = \"#3498DB\")) +\n    theme_bw() +\n    labs(title = \"GO Enrichment (BP + CC + MF)\", x = \"Gene Count\", y = \"\") +\n    theme(plot.title = element_text(hjust = 0.5, face = \"bold\"),\n          axis.text.y = element_text(size = 8))\n  ggsave(file.path(out_dir, \"06_GO_combined_barplot.pdf\"), p_go3, width = 11, height = 8)\n}\n\ncat(\"  GO/KEGG 可视化已保存\\n\")\n\n\n# ╔════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════╗\n# ║  Step 7: Hub 基因识别 (类 CytoHubba)                                      ║\n# ╚════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════╝\n#\n# ┌──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┐\n# │ Cytoscape 操作指南 (手动补充):                                            │\n# │  1. 打开 Cytoscape → File → Import → Network from File                  │\n# │     导入 05_PPI_for_cytoscape.sif                                       │\n# │  2. 安装 CytoHubba 插件: Apps → App Manager → 搜索 cytoHubba           │\n# │  3. 选择 CytoHubba → 选择算法 (Degree, MCC, Betweenness 等)            │\n# │  4. 设置 Top N = 10, 运行                                               │\n# │  5. 交叉多种算法结果, 确定核心 Hub 基因                                   │\n# │                                                                          │\n# │ 下方代码在 R 中模拟 CytoHubba 多指标排序                                 │\n# └──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┘\n\ncat(\"\\n══ Step 7: Hub 基因识别 ══\\n\")\n\nif (vcount(g) < 3) {\n  cat(\"  ⚠ PPI 网络节点过少, 跳过 Hub 基因分析\\n\")\n  hub_genes_final <- V(g)$name\n} else {\n\n  # --- 计算多种中心性指标 ---\n  centrality_df <- data.frame(\n    gene        = V(g)$name,\n    Degree      = degree(g),\n    Betweenness = betweenness(g, normalized = TRUE),\n    Closeness   = closeness(g, normalized = TRUE),\n    Eigenvector = eigen_centrality(g)$vector,\n    PageRank    = page_rank(g)$vector,\n    stringsAsFactors = FALSE\n  )\n\n  # --- MCC (Maximal Clique Centrality, CytoHubba 核心算法) ---\n  cat(\"  计算 MCC (Maximal Clique Centrality)...\\n\")\n  mc <- max_cliques(g)\n  mcc_scores <- sapply(V(g)$name, function(v) {\n    v_idx     <- which(V(g)$name == v)\n    v_cliques <- mc[sapply(mc, function(cl) v_idx %in% cl)]\n    sum(sapply(v_cliques, function(cl) factorial(min(length(cl) - 1, 10))))\n    # 限制 factorial(10) 防止溢出\n  })\n  centrality_df$MCC <- mcc_scores[centrality_df$gene]\n\n  # --- 每个指标取 Top N 并计算出现频次 ---\n  n_top <- min(20, nrow(centrality_df))\n  metrics <- c(\"Degree\", \"Betweenness\", \"Closeness\", \"Eigenvector\", \"PageRank\", \"MCC\")\n  top_lists <- lapply(metrics, function(m) {\n    centrality_df$gene[order(centrality_df[[m]], decreasing = TRUE)][1:n_top]\n  })\n  names(top_lists) <- metrics\n\n  top_freq <- table(unlist(top_lists))\n  top_freq_sorted <- sort(top_freq, decreasing = TRUE)\n\n  # 取出现在 >= 3 个指标 Top 列表中的基因; 如果不足 5 个, 取前 10\n  hub_genes_final <- names(top_freq_sorted[top_freq_sorted >= 3])\n  if (length(hub_genes_final) < 5) {\n    hub_genes_final <- names(top_freq_sorted)[1:min(10, length(top_freq_sorted))]\n  }\n\n  cat(sprintf(\"  Hub 基因 (%d 个): %s\\n\",\n              length(hub_genes_final), paste(hub_genes_final, collapse = \", \")))\n\n  # --- 保存中心性分析和 Hub 基因 ---\n  centrality_sorted <- centrality_df %>% arrange(desc(Degree))\n  write.csv(centrality_sorted, file.path(out_dir, \"07_centrality_all.csv\"), row.names = FALSE)\n\n  hub_detail <- centrality_df %>%\n    filter(gene %in% hub_genes_final) %>%\n    mutate(top_count = as.integer(top_freq_sorted[gene])) %>%\n    arrange(desc(top_count), desc(Degree))\n  write.csv(hub_detail, file.path(out_dir, \"07_hub_genes.csv\"), row.names = FALSE)\n\n  # --- Hub 子网络可视化 ---\n  hub_in_graph <- hub_genes_final[hub_genes_final %in% V(g)$name]\n  if (length(hub_in_graph) >= 2) {\n    g_hub <- induced_subgraph(g, hub_in_graph)\n\n    pdf(file.path(out_dir, \"07_hub_gene_network.pdf\"), width = 10, height = 10)\n    set.seed(42)\n    V(g_hub)$size      <- rescale(degree(g_hub), to = c(18, 40))\n    V(g_hub)$color     <- colorRampPalette(c(\"#FEE08B\", \"#E74C3C\"))(vcount(g_hub))\n    V(g_hub)$label.cex <- 1.3\n    V(g_hub)$frame.color <- \"grey30\"\n    plot(g_hub,\n         layout = layout_with_fr(g_hub),\n         vertex.label.color = \"black\",\n         edge.color = \"grey50\", edge.width = 2,\n         main = paste0(\"Hub Gene Network (Top \", length(hub_in_graph), \")\"))\n    dev.off()\n    cat(\"  已保存: 07_hub_gene_network.pdf\\n\")\n  }\n\n  # --- Hub 基因中心性指标柱状图 ---\n  hub_long <- hub_detail %>%\n    select(gene, Degree, Betweenness, Closeness, MCC) %>%\n    pivot_longer(-gene, names_to = \"Metric\", values_to = \"Value\")\n\n  # 每个指标单独缩放到 0-1\n  hub_long <- hub_long %>%\n    group_by(Metric) %>%\n    mutate(Value_scaled = rescale(Value)) %>%\n    ungroup()\n\n  p_hub_bar <- ggplot(hub_long, aes(x = reorder(gene, -Value_scaled), y = Value_scaled, fill = Metric)) +\n    geom_col(position = \"dodge\", width = 0.7) +\n    facet_wrap(~Metric, scales = \"free_y\", ncol = 2) +\n    theme_bw() +\n    labs(title = \"Hub Gene Centrality Metrics\", x = \"\", y = \"Scaled Value\") +\n    theme(axis.text.x = element_text(angle = 45, hjust = 1, size = 9),\n          plot.title = element_text(hjust = 0.5, face = \"bold\"),\n          legend.position = \"none\")\n  ggsave(file.path(out_dir, \"07_hub_centrality_barplot.pdf\"), p_hub_bar,\n         width = 10, height = 8)\n}\n\n\n# ╔════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════╗\n# ║  Step 8: Hub 基因表达验证                                                  ║\n# ╚════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════╝\n\ncat(\"\\n══ Step 8: Hub 基因表达验证 ══\\n\")\n\n# --- 读取表达矩阵和样本信息 ---\nexp_mat <- read.csv(\"exp.csv\", row.names = 1, check.names = FALSE)\npd      <- read.csv(\"pd.csv\", row.names = 1, check.names = FALSE)\n\n# 样本分组 (Young/Aged × sham/MCAO)\npd$group <- paste(\n  ifelse(grepl(\"3-4 months\", pd[[\"age:ch1\"]]), \"Young\", \"Aged\"),\n  pd[[\"treatment:ch1\"]],\n  sep = \"_\"\n)\ncat(\"  样本分组:\\n\")\nprint(table(pd$group))\n\n# --- Hub 基因: 人类符号 → 大鼠符号映射 ---\nto_rat_symbol <- function(human) {\n  s <- tolower(human)\n  paste0(toupper(substr(s, 1, 1)), substr(s, 2, nchar(s)))\n}\n\n# 构建映射表\nhub_map <- data.frame(\n  human = hub_genes_final,\n  rat   = sapply(hub_genes_final, to_rat_symbol),\n  stringsAsFactors = FALSE\n)\n\n# 在表达矩阵中查找 (尝试多种匹配)\nhub_map$in_exp <- NA\nfor (i in seq_len(nrow(hub_map))) {\n  h <- hub_map$human[i]\n  r <- hub_map$rat[i]\n\n  if (r %in% rownames(exp_mat)) {\n    hub_map$in_exp[i] <- r\n  } else if (h %in% rownames(exp_mat)) {\n    hub_map$in_exp[i] <- h\n  } else {\n    # 模糊匹配 (忽略大小写)\n    idx <- grep(paste0(\"^\", r, \"$\"), rownames(exp_mat), ignore.case = TRUE)\n    if (length(idx) > 0) hub_map$in_exp[i] <- rownames(exp_mat)[idx[1]]\n  }\n}\n\nhub_found <- hub_map %>% filter(!is.na(in_exp))\ncat(sprintf(\"  Hub 基因在表达矩阵中匹配: %d / %d\\n\", nrow(hub_found), nrow(hub_map)))\n\nif (nrow(hub_found) > 0) {\n  cat(\"  匹配到:\", paste(hub_found$in_exp, collapse = \", \"), \"\\n\")\n}\n\nif (nrow(hub_found) == 0) {\n  cat(\"  ⚠ 未在表达矩阵中找到任何 Hub 基因。\\n\")\n  cat(\"    可能原因: 基因符号格式差异或物种映射问题\\n\")\n} else {\n\n  # 提取 Hub 基因表达\n  hub_exp <- exp_mat[hub_found$in_exp, , drop = FALSE]\n\n  # 确保样本顺序一致\n  common_samples <- intersect(colnames(hub_exp), rownames(pd))\n  hub_exp <- hub_exp[, common_samples, drop = FALSE]\n  pd_sub  <- pd[common_samples, , drop = FALSE]\n\n  # ── 热图 ──\n  anno_col <- data.frame(\n    Group = pd_sub$group,\n    row.names = common_samples\n  )\n\n  group_colors <- c(\n    \"Young_sham\" = \"#3498DB\", \"Aged_sham\" = \"#27AE60\",\n    \"Young_MCAO\" = \"#F39C12\", \"Aged_MCAO\" = \"#E74C3C\"\n  )\n  ann_colors <- list(Group = group_colors[sort(unique(pd_sub$group))])\n\n  # 行标签: 大鼠名 (人类名)\n  row_labels <- paste0(hub_found$in_exp, \" (\", hub_found$human, \")\")\n\n  pdf(file.path(out_dir, \"08_hub_gene_heatmap.pdf\"),\n      width = 10, height = max(5, nrow(hub_found) * 0.5 + 2))\n  pheatmap(\n    as.matrix(hub_exp),\n    annotation_col  = anno_col,\n    annotation_colors = ann_colors,\n    labels_row      = row_labels,\n    scale           = \"row\",\n    cluster_cols    = FALSE,\n    show_colnames   = FALSE,\n    color           = colorRampPalette(c(\"#3498DB\", \"white\", \"#E74C3C\"))(100),\n    fontsize_row    = 10,\n    main            = \"Hub Gene Expression Heatmap\"\n  )\n  dev.off()\n  cat(\"  已保存: 08_hub_gene_heatmap.pdf\\n\")\n\n  # ── Boxplot ──\n  plot_df <- hub_exp %>%\n    as.data.frame() %>%\n    rownames_to_column(\"gene_rat\") %>%\n    pivot_longer(-gene_rat, names_to = \"sample\", values_to = \"expression\") %>%\n    left_join(hub_found %>% rename(gene_rat = in_exp), by = \"gene_rat\") %>%\n    mutate(\n      group      = pd[sample, \"group\"],\n      gene_label = paste0(gene_rat, \" (\", human, \")\")\n    )\n\n  # 指定分组顺序\n  plot_df$group <- factor(plot_df$group,\n                          levels = c(\"Young_sham\", \"Aged_sham\", \"Young_MCAO\", \"Aged_MCAO\"))\n\n  ncol_facet <- min(4, nrow(hub_found))\n  nrow_facet <- ceiling(nrow(hub_found) / ncol_facet)\n\n  p_box <- ggplot(plot_df, aes(x = group, y = expression, fill = group)) +\n    geom_boxplot(outlier.shape = NA, alpha = 0.7, width = 0.6) +\n    geom_jitter(width = 0.12, size = 2, alpha = 0.8) +\n    facet_wrap(~gene_label, scales = \"free_y\", ncol = ncol_facet) +\n    scale_fill_manual(values = group_colors) +\n    theme_bw() +\n    theme(\n      axis.text.x    = element_text(angle = 45, hjust = 1, size = 8),\n      strip.text     = element_text(face = \"bold\", size = 9),\n      legend.position = \"none\"\n    ) +\n    labs(title = \"Hub Gene Expression Validation (GSE166162)\",\n         x = \"\", y = \"Expression Level\")\n\n  ggsave(file.path(out_dir, \"08_hub_gene_boxplot.pdf\"), p_box,\n         width = ncol_facet * 3.5 + 1, height = nrow_facet * 3.5 + 1)\n  cat(\"  已保存: 08_hub_gene_boxplot.pdf\\n\")\n\n  # ── 统计检验: Aged MCAO vs Aged sham ──\n  stat_results <- lapply(seq_len(nrow(hub_found)), function(i) {\n    gene_r <- hub_found$in_exp[i]\n    gene_h <- hub_found$human[i]\n\n    vals_mcao <- as.numeric(hub_exp[gene_r, pd_sub$group == \"Aged_MCAO\"])\n    vals_sham <- as.numeric(hub_exp[gene_r, pd_sub$group == \"Aged_sham\"])\n\n    if (length(vals_mcao) >= 2 && length(vals_sham) >= 2) {\n      tt <- tryCatch(t.test(vals_mcao, vals_sham), error = function(e) NULL)\n      wt <- tryCatch(wilcox.test(vals_mcao, vals_sham), error = function(e) NULL)\n\n      data.frame(\n        gene_human  = gene_h,\n        gene_rat    = gene_r,\n        mean_MCAO   = mean(vals_mcao),\n        mean_sham   = mean(vals_sham),\n        logFC       = log2(mean(vals_mcao) / mean(vals_sham)),\n        t_pvalue    = if (!is.null(tt)) tt$p.value else NA,\n        wilcox_pvalue = if (!is.null(wt)) wt$p.value else NA,\n        stringsAsFactors = FALSE\n      )\n    } else {\n      NULL\n    }\n  })\n\n  stat_df <- bind_rows(stat_results) %>% arrange(t_pvalue)\n  write.csv(stat_df, file.path(out_dir, \"08_hub_gene_validation_stats.csv\"), row.names = FALSE)\n  cat(\"  已保存: 08_hub_gene_validation_stats.csv\\n\")\n\n  # 打印验证结果\n  cat(\"\\n  ── Hub 基因验证 (Aged MCAO vs Aged sham) ──\\n\")\n  print(stat_df, row.names = FALSE)\n}\n\n\n# ╔════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════╗\n# ║  分析完成! 输出文件汇总                                                    ║\n# ╚════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════╝\n\ncat(\"\\n\")\ncat(\"═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════\\n\")\ncat(\"  网络药理学分析 Pipeline 完成!\\n\")\ncat(\"═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════\\n\")\ncat(\"  输出目录:\", out_dir, \"\\n\\n\")\n\nall_files <- list.files(out_dir, full.names = FALSE)\ncat(\"  生成文件:\\n\")\nfor (f in all_files) {\n  cat(\"    \", f, \"\\n\")\n}\n\ncat(\"\\n\")\ncat(\"  后续可在 Cytoscape 中进一步分析:\\n\")\ncat(\"    1. File → Import → Network from File → 05_PPI_for_cytoscape.sif\\n\")\ncat(\"    2. Apps → cytoHubba → 选择 MCC/Degree/Betweenness 等算法\\n\")\ncat(\"    3. 与本脚本 Step 7 结果交叉验证 Hub 基因\\n\")\ncat(\"═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════\\n\")\n"

脚本已创建并通过语法检查：[network_pharmacology_pipeline.R](test/00_GEO_data_GSE166162/network_pharmacology_pipeline.R)

**脚本包含 8 个步骤，全流程覆盖：**

| 步骤 | 内容 | 说明 |
|------|------|------|
| 1 | DEG 筛选 | P.Value < 0.05, \|logFC\| ≥ 1, 大鼠→人类符号转换 + 火山图 |
| 2 | 疾病基因 | Open Targets API 自动获取 (Ischemic Stroke), 失败可手动放 GeneCards CSV |
| 3 | 中药靶点 | 读取 TCMSP 手动下载的 CSV (已生成模板), 含 6 味药搜索名对照表 |
| 4 | Venn 交集 | DEG ∩ 疾病 ∩ 中药, 交集不足自动降级为 DEG ∩ (疾病 ∪ 中药) |
| 5 | PPI 网络 | STRING REST API + STRINGdb R包双通道, 导出 Cytoscape SIF |
| 6 | GO/KEGG | clusterProfiler, BP/CC/MF dotplot + barplot + 三合一图 |
| 7 | Hub 基因 | Degree/Betweenness/Closeness/Eigenvector/PageRank/MCC 六指标排序 |
| 8 | 表达验证 | 热图 + 分组 Boxplot + t检验/Wilcoxon 统计 (Aged MCAO vs Aged sham) |

**需要手动准备的文件（第一次运行会在 network_pharmacology/ 下生成模板）：**
- 03_herb_targets.csv — 从 TCMSP 下载 6 味中药的靶点基因（脚本中有详细搜索名对照）
- 02_disease_genes.csv — 如 API 失败则需从 GeneCards 下载

所有输出保存在 network_pharmacology/ 子目录。

bind_rows(all_interactions)\n    df <- df %>%\n      select(preferredName_A, preferredName_B, score) %>%\n      rename(gene1 = preferredName_A, gene2 = preferredName_B, combined_score = score) %>%\n      distinct()\n    return(df)\n  }\n  return(NULL)\n}\n\n# --- 方法 B: STRINGdb R 包 ---\nbuild_ppi_from_pkg <- function(genes, species = 9606, score_threshold = 400) {\n  tryCatch({\n    sdb    <- STRINGdb$new(version = \"12.0\", species = species,\n                           score_threshold = score_threshold, network_type = \"full\")\n    gene_df <- data.frame(gene = genes, stringsAsFactors = FALSE)\n    mapped  <- sdb$map(gene_df, \"gene\", removeUnmappedRows = TRUE)\n\n    if (nrow(mapped) < 2) return(NULL)\n\n    interactions <- sdb$get_interactions(mapped$STRING_id)\n    if (nrow(interactions) == 0) return(NULL)\n\n    id2gene <- setNames(mapped$gene, mapped$STRING_id)\n    interactions %>%\n      mutate(gene1 = id2gene[from], gene2 = id2gene[to]) %>%\n      filter(!is.na(gene1), !is.na(gene2)) %>%\n      select(gene1, gene2, combined_score)\n  }, error = function(e) {\n    message(\"    STRINGdb R 包查询失败: \", conditionMessage(e))\n    NULL\n  })\n}\n\n# 先尝试 REST API, 失败则用 R 包\ncat(\"  正在查询 STRING (REST API)...\\n\")\nppi_df <- build_ppi_from_rest(target_genes)\n\nif (is.null(ppi_df) || nrow(ppi_df) == 0) {\n  cat(\"  REST API 无结果, 尝试 STRINGdb R 包...\\n\")\n  ppi_df <- build_ppi_from_pkg(target_genes)\n}\n\nif (is.null(ppi_df) || nrow(ppi_df) == 0) {\n  cat(\"  !! STRING 未返回互作数据。可能原因:\\n\")\n  cat(\"     1. 网络连接问题\\n\")\n  cat(\"     2. 交集基因在 STRING 中无互作\\n\")\n  cat(\"  → 请手动到 https://string-db.org/ 输入基因列表查询,\\n\")\n  cat(\"    导出 TSV 保存为:\", file.path(out_dir, \"06_PPI_interactions.csv\"), \"\\n\")\n  cat(\"    列名: gene1, gene2, combined_score\\n\")\n\n  # 尝试读取用户手动上传的文件\n  manual_ppi <- file.path(out_dir, \"06_PPI_interactions.csv\")\n  if (file.exists(manual_ppi)) {\n    ppi_df <- read.csv(manual_ppi, stringsAsFactors = FALSE)\n    cat(\"  从手动文件读取 PPI 数据\\n\")\n  } else {\n    stop(\"无法获取 PPI 数据, 请检查网络或手动下载\")\n  }\n}\n\ncat(sprintf(\"  PPI 互作边数: %d\\n\", nrow(ppi_df)))\n\n# 保存 PPI (可导入 Cytoscape)\nwrite.csv(ppi_df, file.path(out_dir, \"06_PPI_interactions.csv\"), row.names = FALSE)\n\n# 导出 Cytoscape SIF 格式\nwrite.table(\n  ppi_df[, c(\"gene1\", \"gene2\")],\n  file.path(out_dir, \"06_PPI_for_cytoscape.sif\"),\n  sep = \"\\t\", row.names = FALSE, col.names = FALSE, quote = FALSE\n)\n\n# --- 用 igraph 构建网络 ---\ng <- graph_from_data_frame(ppi_df[, c(\"gene1\", \"gene2\")], directed = FALSE)\ng <- simplify(g)\n\n# 删除孤立节点\niso <- which(degree(g) == 0)\nif (length(iso) > 0) g <- delete_vertices(g, iso)\n\nV(g)$degree <- degree(g)\n\ncat(sprintf(\"  PPI 网络: %d 节点, %d 边\\n\", vcount(g), ecount(g)))\n\n# --- PPI 网络可视化 ---\npdf(file.path(out_dir, \"06_PPI_network_plot.pdf\"), width = 14, height = 14)\nset.seed(42)\nn_colors   <- max(V(g)$degree, na.rm = TRUE)\npal        <- colorRampPalette(c(\"#5DADE2\", \"#F4D03F\", \"#E74C3C\"))(n_colors + 1)\nV(g)$color <- pal[V(g)$degree + 1]\nV(g)$size  <- rescale(V(g)$degree, to = c(5, 22))\nV(g)$label.cex <- rescale(V(g)$degree, to = c(0.5, 1.3))\nV(g)$frame.color <- NA\n\nplot(g,\n     layout          = layout_with_fr(g),\n     vertex.label.color = \"grey10\",\n     edge.color      = adjustcolor(\"grey60\", alpha.f = 0.5),\n     edge.width      = 0.8,\n     main            = paste0(\"PPI Network (\", vcount(g), \" nodes, \", ecount(g), \" edges)\"))\ndev.off()\ncat(\"  已保存: 06_PPI_network_plot.pdf\\n\")"
}

现在用 JavaScript 把淫羊藿数据以 JSON 形式保存，然后批量处理。让我写一个方案：把所有 6 味药的数据用浏览器自动化提取，然后用 R 脚本做 UniProt 映射。先把淫羊藿的 511 条记录写入文件：

▸ Tool calls (1)
mcp_microsoft_pla_browser_evaluate 
{
  "function": "() => { var grid0 = $(document.querySelectorAll('[data-role=\"grid\"]')[0]).data('kendoGrid'); grid0.dataSource.pageSize(9999); var grid1 = $(document.querySelectorAll('[data-role=\"grid\"]')[1]).data('kendoGrid'); grid1.dataSource.pageSize(9999); var ingr = grid0.dataSource.data(); var targ = grid1.dataSource.data(); var activeIDs = new Set(); for (var i = 0; i < ingr.length; i++) { if (ingr[i].ob >= 30 && ingr[i].dl >= 0.18) activeIDs.add(ingr[i].MOL_ID); } var lines = []; var seen = new Set(); for (var j = 0; j < targ.length; j++) { if (activeIDs.has(targ[j].MOL_ID)) { var key = targ[j].MOL_ID + '|' + targ[j].target_name; if (!seen.has(key)) { seen.add(key); lines.push(targ[j].MOL_ID + '\\t' + targ[j].molecule_name.replace(/[\\t\\n]/g,' ') + '\\t' + targ[j].target_name.replace(/[\\t\\n]/g,' ') + '\\t' + targ[j].drugbank_ID); } } } return lines.join('\\n'); }"
}

API 工作正常。编写批量映射脚本：

▸ Tool calls (1)
run_in_terminal 
{
  "command": "cd /Users/yuzuan/Desktop/fastGEO/test/00_GEO_data_GSE166162/network_pharmacology && python3 << 'PYEOF'\nimport urllib.request, urllib.parse, time, sys\n\nwith open('tcmsp_unique_proteins.txt') as f:\n    proteins = [line.strip() for line in f if line.strip()]\n\nprint(f\"Total proteins to map: {len(proteins)}\")\n\nresults = {}\nfailed = []\n\nfor i, pname in enumerate(proteins):\n    query = f'(protein_name:\"{pname}\") AND (organism_id:9606) AND (reviewed:true)'\n    params = urllib.parse.urlencode({\n        'query': query,\n        'fields': 'gene_primary',\n        'format': 'tsv',\n        'size': '1'\n    })\n    url = f'https://rest.uniprot.org/uniprotkb/search?{params}'\n    \n    try:\n        req = urllib.request.Request(url, headers={'User-Agent': 'Python/3'})\n        with urllib.request.urlopen(req, timeout=10) as resp:\n            text = resp.read().decode('utf-8').strip()\n            lines = text.split('\\n')\n            if len(lines) >= 2:\n                gene = lines[1].strip()\n                if gene:\n                    results[pname] = gene\n                else:\n                    failed.append(pname)\n            else:\n                failed.append(pname)\n    except Exception as e:\n        failed.append(pname)\n    \n    if (i+1) % 50 == 0:\n        print(f\"  Processed {i+1}/{len(proteins)}, mapped: {len(results)}, failed: {len(failed)}\")\n    \n    time.sleep(0.2)  # Rate limiting\n\nprint(f\"\\nDone! Mapped: {len(results)}, Failed: {len(failed)}\")\n\n# Save mapping\nwith open('protein_to_gene_map.tsv', 'w') as f:\n    f.write('protein_name\\tgene_symbol\\n')\n    for pname, gene in sorted(results.items()):\n        f.write(f'{pname}\\t{gene}\\n')\n\n# Save failed\nif failed:\n    with open('protein_mapping_failed.txt', 'w') as f:\n        for p in failed:\n            f.write(p + '\\n')\n    print(f\"Failed proteins saved to protein_mapping_failed.txt\")\n    print(\"First 10 failed:\", failed[:10])\n\nPYEOF",
  "explanation": "批量查询 UniProt 将 251 个蛋白名映射为基因符号",
  "goal": "UniProt 蛋白→基因映射",
  "mode": "sync",
  "timeout": 300000

- **交集基因**: 20 个（DEG ∩ 疾病基因 ∩ 药物靶点），比之前模板数据的 13 个增加了 7 个新基因：**SPP1, CDK1, CCNA2, CD14, JUNB, FOS, CLEC7A**

▸ Tool calls (1)
run_in_terminal 
{
  "command": "cd /Users/yuzuan/Desktop/fastGEO/test/00_GEO_data_GSE166162 && Rscript -e '\nsuppressPackageStartupMessages({\n  library(pheatmap)\n  library(ggplotify)\n  library(ggplot2)\n})\n\n# 读数据\nexp <- read.csv(\"exp.csv\", row.names = 1, check.names = FALSE)\ndeg_all <- read.csv(\"GSE166162_DEG.csv\", row.names = 1, check.names = FALSE)\npd <- read.csv(\"pd.csv\", row.names = 1, check.names = FALSE)\n\n# 重新标记 DEG 方向 (P.Value < 0.05, |logFC| >= 1)\ndeg_all$DEG <- \"Not_Change\"\ndeg_all$DEG[deg_all$P.Value < 0.05 & deg_all$logFC >= 1] <- \"Up\"\ndeg_all$DEG[deg_all$P.Value < 0.05 & deg_all$logFC <= -1] <- \"Down\"\ncat(\"DEG table:\", table(deg_all$DEG), \"\\n\")\n\n# 分组: Aged_MCAO vs Aged_Sham (用比较组)\npd$group <- paste0(\n  ifelse(grepl(\"Young\", pd$title), \"Young\", \"Aged\"), \"_\",\n  ifelse(grepl(\"sham\", pd$title), \"Sham\", \"MCAO\")\n)\ncat(\"Groups:\", table(pd$group), \"\\n\")\n# 比较: Aged_MCAO vs Aged_Sham\ncase <- \"Aged_MCAO\"\ncontrol <- \"Aged_Sham\"\n\n# 按 logFC 排序, 取 top 20 Up + top 20 Down\ndeg_sorted <- deg_all[order(deg_all$logFC, decreasing = TRUE), ]\ndeg_up <- deg_sorted[deg_sorted$DEG == \"Up\", ]\ndeg_dn <- deg_sorted[deg_sorted$DEG == \"Down\", ]\nntop <- 20\nUP_top <- head(rownames(deg_up), ntop)\nDN_top <- tail(rownames(deg_dn), ntop)\ncat(\"Up top:\", length(UP_top), \" Down top:\", length(DN_top), \"\\n\")\n\n# 取子集表达矩阵: 按组排列列\nSID_case <- rownames(pd)[pd$group == case]\nSID_ctrl <- rownames(pd)[pd$group == control]\npdata <- exp[c(UP_top, DN_top), c(SID_ctrl, SID_case)]\n\n# 注释\nannotation_col <- data.frame(\n  Group = c(rep(control, length(SID_ctrl)), rep(case, length(SID_case))),\n  row.names = c(SID_ctrl, SID_case)\n)\nannotation_row <- data.frame(\n  DEG = c(rep(\"Up\", length(UP_top)), rep(\"Down\", length(DN_top))),\n  row.names = c(UP_top, DN_top)\n)\n\n# fastGEO 风格颜色\nmy_cols1 <- c(\"#1C79B7\", \"#F38329\", \"#2DA248\", \"#DC403E\", \"#976BA6\")\nannotation_colors <- list(\n  Group = c(Aged_Sham = my_cols1[1], Aged_MCAO = my_cols1[2]),\n  DEG = c(Up = my_cols1[4], Down = my_cols1[1])\n)\n\n# 绘制 fastGEO 风格热图\np <- pheatmap(\n  pdata,\n  scale = \"row\",\n  show_rownames = TRUE,\n  show_colnames = FALSE,\n  cluster_cols = FALSE,\n  cluster_rows = FALSE,\n  annotation_col = annotation_col,\n  annotation_row = annotation_row,\n  annotation_colors = annotation_colors,\n  border_color = NA,\n  gaps_row = length(UP_top),\n  gaps_col = length(SID_ctrl),\n  color = colorRampPalette(c(\"blue\", \"white\", \"red\"))(50),\n  annotation_names_col = FALSE,\n  annotation_names_row = FALSE,\n  silent = TRUE,\n  fontsize_row = 7\n)\n\np_gg <- ggplotify::as.ggplot(p) + theme(plot.margin = margin(l = 5, r = 10))\nggsave(file.path(\"network_pharmacology\", \"DEG_heatmap_fastGEO.pdf\"), p_gg, width = 6, height = 8)\nggsave(file.path(\"network_pharmacology\", \"DEG_heatmap_fastGEO.png\"), p_gg, width = 6, height = 8, dpi = 300)\ncat(\"✅ 已保存: DEG_heatmap_fastGEO.pdf / .png\\n\")\n' 2>&1",

4. Comment blocks that are purely instructions/notes (like the Step 2 GeneCards manual download block, Step 3 TCMSP block) become Markdown paragraphs OUTSIDE code chunks
5. For figure chunks, add appropriate fig.width and fig.height in chunk options
6. Keep ALL code exactly as-is — do NOT modify any R code logic, variable names, function calls, or comments within code
7. Use message=FALSE, warning=FALSE for the setup/package-loading chunk

查询函数: Open Targets ---\nquery_opentargets <- function(efo_id, size = 5000) {\n  tryCatch({\n    url   <- \"https://api.platform.opentargets.org/api/v4/graphql\"\n    query <- sprintf('{\n      disease(efoId: \"%s\") {\n        name\n        associatedTargets(page: {index: 0, size: %d}) {\n          count\n          rows { target { approvedSymbol } score }\n        }\n      }\n    }', efo_id, size)\n\n    res <- httr::POST(url,\n                body = toJSON(list(query = query), auto_unbox = TRUE),\n                httr::content_type_json(), httr::timeout(60))\n    if (httr::status_code(res) != 200) return(NULL)\n\n    data <- fromJSON(httr::content(res, as = \"text\", encoding = \"UTF-8\"))\n    rows <- data$data$disease$associatedTargets$rows\n    if (is.null(rows) || length(rows) == 0) return(NULL)\n\n    data.frame(\n      gene_symbol = rows$target$approvedSymbol,\n      score       = rows$score,\n      stringsAsFactors = FALSE\n    )\n  }, error = function(e) {\n    message(\"    Open Targets 查询失败: \", conditionMessage(e))\n    NULL\n  })\n}\n\n# --- API 查询函数: STRING REST (补充搜索 Aging 相关基因) ---\nquery_string_disease <- function(disease_term, species = 9606, limit = 500) {\n  tryCatch({\n    url <- paste0(\n      \"https://string-db.org/api/json/enrichment?\",\n      \"identifiers=\", URLencode(disease_term),\n      \"&species=\", species\n    )\n    # STRING 没有直接的疾病-基因接口; 此处仅做占位, 主要依赖 Open Targets\n    NULL\n  }, error = function(e) NULL)\n}\n```\n\n## 2.2 获取疾病基因\n\n```{r get_disease_genes}\ndisease_genes_file \"bold\"))\n\nggsave(file.path(out_dir, \"04_venn_diagram.pdf\"), p_venn, width = 8, height = 7)\ncat(\"  已保存: 04_venn_diagram.pdf\\n\")\n\np_venn\n```\n\n\n# Step 5: GO / KEGG 富集分析\n\n## 5.1 基因 ID 转换与富集\n\n```{r enrichment_analysis}\ncat(\"\\n══ Step 5: GO / KEGG 富集分析 ══\\n\")\n\n# 基因 Symbol → Entrez ID\ngene_ids <- bitr(target_genes, fromType = \"SYMBOL\", toType = \"ENTREZID\",\n                 OrgDb = org.Hs.eg.db)\ncat(sprintf(\"  SYMBOL → ENTREZ 转换: %d / %d\\n\", nrow(gene_ids), length(target_genes)))\n\nentrez_list <- unique(gene_ids$ENTREZID)\n\n# --- GO 富集 ---\nego_bp <- enrichGO(gene = entrez_list, OrgDb = org.Hs.eg.db, ont = \"BP\",\n                   pAdjustMethod = \"BH\", pvalueCutoff = 0.05, qvalueCutoff = 0.2,\n                   readable = TRUE)\nego_cc <- enrichGO(gene = entrez_list, OrgDb = org.Hs.eg.db, ont = \"CC\",\n                   pAdjustMethod = \"BH\", pvalueCutoff = 0.05, qvalueCutoff = 0.2,\n                   readable = TRUE)\nego_mf <- enrichGO(gene = entrez_list, OrgDb = org.Hs.eg.db, ont = \"MF\",\n                   pAdjustMethod = \"BH\", pvalueCutoff = 0.05, qvalueCutoff = 0.2,\n                   readable = TRUE)\n\n# --- KEGG 富集 ---\nekegg <- enrichKEGG(gene = entrez_list, organism = \"hsa\",\n                    pvalueCutoff = 0.05, qvalueCutoff = 0.2)\n\n# --- 保存 CSV ---\ngo_kegg_results <- list(\n  GO_BP = ego_bp, GO_CC = ego_cc, GO_MF = ego_mf, KEGG = ekegg\n)\nfor (nm in names(go_kegg_results)) {\n  obj <- go_kegg_results[[nm]]\n  if (!is.null(obj) && nrow(as.data.frame(obj)) > 0) {\n    write.csv(as.data.frame(obj), file.path(out_dir, paste0(\"05_\", nm, \".csv\")), row.names = FALSE)\n    cat(sprintf(\"  %s: %d 条显著通路\\n\", nm, nrow(as.data.frame(obj))))\n  } else {\n    cat(sprintf(\"  %s: 无显著结果\\n\", nm))\n  }\n}\n```\n\n## 5.2 GO BP 可视化\n\n```{r go_bp_plots, fig.width=10, fig.height=9}\nif (!is.null(ego_bp) && nrow(as.data.frame(ego_bp)) > 0) {\n  p1 <- print(p1)\n}\n```\n\n## 5.3 GO CC 可视化\n\n```{r go_cc_plot, fig.width=10, fig.height=8}\nif (!is.null(ego_cc) && nrow(as.data.frame(ego_cc)) > 0) {\n  p2 <- dotplot(ego_cc, showCategory = 15, title = fig.height=8}\ncombine_go_top <- function(bp, cc, mf, top_n = 5) {\n  dfs <- list()\n  if (!is.null(bp) && nrow(as.data.frame(bp)) > 0)\n    dfs[[\"BP\"]] <- as.data.frame(bp) %>% head(top_n) %>% dplyr::mutate(Category = \"BP\")\n  if (!is.null(cc) && nrow(as.data.frame(cc)) > 0)\n    dfs[[\"CC\"]] <- as.data.frame(cc) %>% head(top_n) %>% dplyr::mutate(Category = \"CC\")\n  if (!is.null(mf) && nrow(as.data.frame(mf)) > 0)\n    dfs[[\"MF\"]] <- as.data.frame(mf) %>% head(top_n) %>% dplyr::mutate(Category = \"MF\")\n\n  if (length(dfs) == 0) return(NULL)\n  dplyr::bind_rows(dfs) %>% dplyr::select(Category, Description, Count, p.adjust)\n}\n\ngo_combined <- combine_go_top(ego_bp, ego_cc, ego_mf, top_n = 8)\nif (!is.null(go_combined) && nrow(go_combined) > 0) {\n  go_combined$Description <- factor(go_combined$Description,\n                                    levels = rev(go_combined$Description))\n  p_go3 <- ggplot(go_combined, aes(Count, Description, fill = Category)) +\n    geom_col(width = 0.7) +\n    scale_fill_manual(values = c(BP = \"#E74C3C\", CC = \"#27AE60\", MF = \"#3498DB\")) +\n    theme_bw() +\n    labs(title = \"GO Enrichment (BP + CC + MF)\", x = \"Gene Count\", y = \"\") +\n    theme(plot.title = element_text(hjust = 0.5, face = \"bold\"),\n          axis.text.y = element_text(size = 8))\n  ggsave(file.path(out_dir, \"05_GO_combined_barplot.pdf\"), p_go3, width = 11, height = 8)\n\n  print(p_go3)\n}\n\ncat(\"  GO/KEGG 可视化已保存\\n\")\n```\n\n\n# Step 6: STRING PPI 网络\n\n## 6.1 PPI 查询函数\n\n```{r ppi_functions}\ncat(\"\\n══ Step 6: PPI 网络 (STRING) ══\\n\")\n\n# --- 方法 A: STRING REST API (更稳定) ---\nbuild_ppi_from_rest <- function(genes, species = 9606, score_threshold = 400) {\n  # 分批查询 (STRING 限制每次 2000 个基因)\n  batch_size <- 500\n  all_interactions <- list()\n\n  for (i in seq(1, length(genes), by = batch_size)) {\n    batch <- genes[i:min(i + batch_size - 1, length(genes))]\n    url   <- \"https://string-db.org/api/json/network\"\n    res   <- tryCatch(\n      httr::GET(url, query = list(\n        identifiers    = paste(batch, collapse = \"\\r\"),\n        species        = species,\n        required_score = score_threshold,\n        caller_identity = \"network_pharmacology_R\"\n      ), httr::timeout(120)),\n      error = function(e) NULL\n    )\n\n    if (!is.null(res) && httr::status_code(res) == 200) {\n      data <- fromJSON(httr::content(res, as = \"text\", encoding = \"UTF-8\"))\n      if (is.data.frame(data) && nrow(data) > 0) {\n        all_interactions[[length(all_interactions) + 1]] <- data\n      }\n    }\n    Sys.sleep(1)  # 礼貌延迟\n  }\n\n  if (length(all_interactions) > 0) {\n    df <- dplyr::bind_rows(all_interactions)\n    df <- df %>%\n      dplyr::select(preferredName_A, preferredName_B, score) %>%\n      dplyr::rename(gene1 = preferredName_A, gene2 = preferredName_B, combined_score = score) %>%\n      dplyr::distinct()\n    return(df)\n  }\n  return(NULL)\n}\n\n# --- 方法 B: STRINGdb R 包 ---\nbuild_ppi_from_pkg <- function(genes, species = 9606, score_threshold = 400) {\n  tryCatch({\n    sdb    <- STRINGdb$new(version = \"12.0\", species = species,\n                           score_threshold = score_threshold, network_type = \"full\")\n    gene_df <- data.frame(gene = genes, stringsAsFactors = FALSE)\n    mapped  <- sdb$map(gene_df, \"gene\", removeUnmappedRows = TRUE)\n\n    if (nrow(mapped) < 2) return(NULL)\n\n    interactions <- sdb$get_interactions(mapped$STRING_id)\n    if (nrow(interactions) == 0) return(NULL)\n\n    id2gene <- setNames(mapped$gene, mapped$STRING_id)\n    interactions %>%\n      dplyr::mutate(gene1 = id2gene[from], gene2 = id2gene[to]) %>%\n      dplyr::filter(!is.na(gene1), !is.na(gene2)) %>%\n      dplyr::select(gene1, gene2, combined_score)\n  }, error = function(e) {\n    message(\"    STRINGdb R 包查询失败: \", conditionMessage(e))\n    NULL\n  })\n}\n```\n\n## 6.2 获取 PPI 数据\n\n```{r get_ppi_data}\n# 先尝试 REST API, 失败则用 R 包\ncat(\"  正在查询 STRING (REST API)...\\n\")\nppi_df <- build_ppi_from_rest(target_genes)\n\nif (is.null(ppi_df) || nrow(ppi_df) == 0) {\n  cat(\"  REST API 无结果, 尝试 STRINGdb R 包...\\n\")\n  ppi_df <- build_ppi_from_pkg(target_genes)\n}\n\nif (is.null(ppi_df) || nrow(ppi_df) == 0) {\n  cat(\"  !! STRING 未返回互作数据。可能原因:\\n\")\n  cat(\"     1. 网络连接问题\\n\")\n  cat(\"     2. 交集基因在 STRING 中无互作\\n\")\n  cat(\"  → 请手动到 https://string-db.org/ 输入基因列表查询,\\n\")\n  cat(\"    导出 TSV 保存为:\", file.path(out_dir, \"06_PPI_interactions.csv\"), \"\\n\")\n  cat(\"    列名: gene1, gene2, combined_score\\n\")\n\n  # 尝试读取用户手动上传的文件\n  manual_ppi <- file.path(out_dir, \"06_PPI_interactions.csv\")\n  if (file.exists(manual_ppi)) {\n    ppi_df <- read.csv(manual_ppi, stringsAsFactors = FALSE)\n    cat(\"  从手动文件读取 PPI 数据\\n\")\n  } else {\n    stop(\"无法获取 PPI 数据, 请检查网络或手动下载\")\n  }\n}\n\ncat(sprintf(\"  PPI 互作边数: %d\\n\", nrow(ppi_df)))\n\n# 保存 PPI (可导入 Cytoscape)\nwrite.csv(ppi_df, file.path(out_dir, \"06_PPI_interactions.csv\"), row.names = FALSE)\n\n# 导出 Cytoscape SIF 格式\nwrite.table(\n  ppi_df[, c(\"gene1\", \"gene2\")],\n  file.path(out_dir, \"06_PPI_for_cytoscape.sif\"),\n  sep = \"\\t\", row.names = FALSE, col.names = FALSE, quote = FALSE\n)\n```\n\n## 6.3 PPI 网络可视化\n\n```{r ppi_network_plot, fig.width=14, fig.height=14}\n# --- 用 igraph 构建网络 ---\ng <- graph_from_data_frame(ppi_df[, c(\"gene1\", \"gene2\")], directed = FALSE)\ng <- igraph::simplify(g)\n\n# 删除孤立节点\niso <- which(degree(g) == 0)\nif (length(iso) > 0) g <- delete_vertices(g, iso)\n\nV(g)$degree <- degree(g)\n\ncat(sprintf(\"  PPI 网络: %d 节点, %d 边\\n\", vcount(g), ecount(g)))\n\n# --- PPI 网络可视化 ---\npdf(file.path(out_dir, \"06_PPI_network_plot.pdf\"), width = 14, height = 14)\nset.seed(42)\nn_colors   <- max(V(g)$degree, na.rm = TRUE)\npal        <- colorRampPalette(c(\"#5DADE2\", \"#F4D03F\", \"#E74C3C\"))(n_colors + 1)\nV(g)$color <- pal[V(g)$degree + 1]\nV(g)$size  <- rescale(V(g)$degree, to = c(5, 22))\nV(g)$label.cex <- rescale(V(g)$degree, to = c(0.5, 1.3))\nV(g)$frame.color <- NA\n\nplot(g,\n     layout          = layout_with_fr(g),\n     vertex.label.color = \"grey10\",\n     edge.color      = adjustcolor(\"grey60\", alpha.f = 0.5),\n     edge.width      = 0.8,\n     main            = paste0(\"PPI Network (\", vcount(g), \" nodes, \", ecount(g), \" edges)\"))\ndev.off()\ncat(\"  已保存: 06_PPI_network_plot.pdf\\n\")\n\n# 再画一次显示在 Rmd 中\nset.seed(42)\nplot(g,\n     layout          = layout_with_fr(g),\n     vertex.label.color = \"grey10\",\n     edge.color      = adjustcolor(\"grey60\", alpha.f = 0.5),\n     edge.width      = 0.8,\n     main            = paste0(\"PPI Network (\", vcount(g), \" nodes, \", ecount(g), \" edges)\"))\n```\n\n\n# Step 7: Hub 基因识别 (类 CytoHubba)\n\n**Cytoscape 操作指南 (手动补充):**\n\n1. 打开 Cytoscape → File → Import → Network from File → 导入 `06_PPI_for_cytoscape.sif`\n2. 安装 CytoHubba 插件: Apps → App Manager → 搜索 cytoHubba\n3. 选择 CytoHubba → 选择算法 (Degree, MCC, Betweenness 等)\n4. 设置 Top N = 10, 运行\n5. 交叉多种算法结果, 确定核心 Hub 基因\n\n下方代码在 R 中模拟 CytoHubba 多指标排序。\n\n## 7.1 计算中心性指标\n\n```{r hub_gene_centrality}\ncat(\"\\n══ Step 7: Hub 基因识别 ══\\n\")\n\nif (vcount(g) < 3) {\n  cat(\"  ⚠ PPI 网络节点过少, 跳过 Hub 基因分析\\n\")\n  hub_genes_final <- V(g)$name\n} else {\n\n  # --- 计算多种中心性指标 ---\n  centrality_df <- data.frame(\n    gene        = V(g)$name,\n    Degree      = degree(g),\n    Betweenness = betweenness(g, normalized = TRUE),\n    Closeness   = closeness(g, normalized = TRUE),\n    Eigenvector = eigen_centrality(g)$vector,\n    PageRank    = page_rank(g)$vector,\n    stringsAsFactors = FALSE\n  )\n\n  # --- MCC (Maximal Clique Centrality, CytoHubba 核心算法) ---\n  cat(\"  计算 MCC (Maximal Clique Centrality)...\\n\")\n  mc <- max_cliques(g)\n  mcc_scores <- sapply(V(g)$name, function(v) {\n    v_idx     <- which(V(g)$name == v)\n    v_cliques <- mc[sapply(mc, function(cl) v_idx %in% cl)]\n    sum(sapply(v_cliques, function(cl) factorial(min(length(cl) - 1, 10))))\n    # 限制 factorial(10) 防止溢出\n  })\n  centrality_df$MCC <- mcc_scores[centrality_df$gene]\n\n  # --- 每个指标取 Top N 并计算出现频次 ---\n  n_top <- min(20, nrow(centrality_df))\n  metrics <- c(\"Degree\", \"Betweenness\", \"Closeness\", \"Eigenvector\", \"PageRank\", \"MCC\")\n  top_lists <- lapply(metrics, function(m) {\n    centrality_df$gene[order(centrality_df[[m]], decreasing = TRUE)][1:n_top]\n  })\n  names(top_lists) <- metrics\n\n  top_freq <- table(unlist(top_lists))\n  top_freq_sorted <- sort(top_freq, decreasing = TRUE)\n\n  # 取出现在 >= 3 个指标 Top 列表中的基因; 如果不足 5 个, 取前 10\n  hub_genes_final <- names(top_freq_sorted[top_freq_sorted >= 3])\n  if (length(hub_genes_final) < 5) {\n    hub_genes_final <- names(top_freq_sorted)[1:min(10, length(top_freq_sorted))]\n  }\n\n  cat(sprintf(\"  Hub 基因 (%d 个): %s\\n\",\n              length(hub_genes_final), paste(hub_genes_final, collapse = \", \")))\n\n  # --- 保存中心性分析和 Hub 基因 ---\n  centrality_sorted <- centrality_df %>% dplyr::arrange(desc(Degree))\n  write.csv(centrality_sorted, file.path(out_dir, \"07_centrality_all.csv\"), row.names = FALSE)\n\n  hub_detail <- centrality_df %>%\n    dplyr::filter(gene %in% hub_genes_final) %>%\n    dplyr::mutate(top_count = as.integer(top_freq_sorted[gene])) %>%\n    dplyr::arrange(desc(top_count), desc(Degree))\n  write.csv(hub_detail, file.path(out_dir, \"07_hub_genes.csv\"), row.names = FALSE)\n}\n```\n\n## 7.2 Hub 子网络可视化\n\n```{r hub_network_plot, fig.width=10, fig.height=10}\nif (exists(\"hub_detail\")) {\n  hub_in_graph <- hub_genes_final[hub_genes_final %in% V(g)$name]\n  if (length(hub_in_graph) >= 2) {\n    g_hub <- induced_subgraph(g, hub_in_graph)\n\n    pdf(file.path(out_dir, \"07_hub_gene_network.pdf\"), width = 10, height = 10)\n    set.seed(42)\n    V(g_hub)$size      <- rescale(degree(g_hub), to = c(18, 40))\n    V(g_hub)$color     <- colorRampPalette(c(\"#FEE08B\", \"#E74C3C\"))(vcount(g_hub))\n    V(g_hub)$label.cex <- 1.3\n    V(g_hub)$frame.color <- \"grey30\"\n    plot(g_hub,\n         layout = layout_with_fr(g_hub),\n         vertex.label.color = \"black\",\n         edge.color = \"grey50\", edge.width = 2,\n         main = paste0(\"Hub Gene Network (Top \", length(hub_in_graph), \")\"))\n    dev.off()\n    cat(\"  已保存: 07_hub_gene_network.pdf\\n\")\n\n    # 再画一次显示在 Rmd 中\n    set.seed(42)\n    V(g_hub)$size      <- rescale(degree(g_hub), to = c(18, 40))\n    V(g_hub)$color     <- colorRampPalette(c(\"#FEE08B\", \"#E74C3C\"))(vcount(g_hub))\n    V(g_hub)$label.cex <- 1.3\n    V(g_hub)$frame.color <- \"grey30\"\n    plot(g_hub,\n         layout = layout_with_fr(g_hub),\n         vertex.label.color = \"black\",\n         edge.color = \"grey50\", edge.width = 2,\n         main = paste0(\"Hub Gene Network (Top \", length(hub_in_graph), \")\"))\n  }\n}\n```\n\n## 7.3 Hub 基因中心性柱状图\n\n```{r hub_centrality_barplot, fig.width=10, fig.height=8}\nif (exists(\"hub_detail\")) {\n  hub_long <- hub_detail %>%\n    dplyr::select(gene, Degree, Betweenness, Closeness, MCC) %>%\n    tidyr::pivot_longer(-gene, names_to = \"Metric\", values_to = \"Value\")\n\n  # 每个指标单独缩放到 0-1\n  hub_long <- hub_long %>%\n    dplyr::group_by(Metric) %>%\n    dplyr::mutate(Value_scaled = rescale(Value)) %>%\n    ungroup()\n\n  p_hub_bar <- ggplot(hub_long, aes(x = reorder(gene, -Value_scaled), y = Value_scaled, fill = Metric)) +\n    geom_col(position = \"dodge\", width = 0.7) +\n    facet_wrap(~Metric, scales = \"free_y\", ncol = 2) +\n    theme_bw() +\n    labs(title = \"Hub Gene Centrality Metrics\", x = \"\", y = \"Scaled Value\") +\n    theme(axis.text.x = element_text(angle = 45, hjust = 1, size = 9),\n          plot.title = element_text(hjust = 0.5, face = \"bold\"),\n          legend.position = \"none\")\n  ggsave(file.path(out_dir, \"07_hub_centrality_barplot.pdf\"), p_hub_bar,\n         width = 10, height = 8)\n\n  print(p_hub_bar)\n}\n```\n\n\n# Step 8: Hub 基因表达验证\n\n## 8.1 读取表达矩阵与样本分组\n\n```{r load_expression}\ncat(\"\\n══ Step 8: Hub 基因表达验证 ══\\n\")\n\n# --- 读取表达矩阵和样本信息 ---\nexp_mat <- read.csv(\"exp.csv\", row.names = 1, check.names = FALSE)\npd      <- read.csv(\"pd.csv\", row.names = 1, check.names = FALSE)\n\n# 样本分组 (Young/Aged × sham/MCAO)\npd$group <- paste(\n  ifelse(grepl(\"3-4 months\", pd[[\"age:ch1\"]]), \"Young\", \"Aged\"),\n  pd[[\"treatment:ch1\"]],\n  sep = \"_\"\n)\ncat(\"  样本分组:\\n\")\nprint(table(pd$group))\n```\n\n## 8.2 基因符号映射\n\n```{r hub_gene_mapping}\n# --- Hub 基因: 人类符号 → 大鼠符号映射 ---\nto_rat_symbol <- function(human) {\n  s <- tolower(human)\n  paste0(toupper(substr(s, 1, 1)), substr(s, 2, nchar(s)))\n}\n\n# 构建映射表\nhub_map <- data.frame(\n  human = hub_genes_final,\n  rat   = sapply(hub_genes_final, to_rat_symbol),\n  stringsAsFactors = FALSE\n)\n\n# 在表达矩阵中查找 (尝试多种匹配)\nhub_map$in_exp <- NA\nfor (i in seq_len(nrow(hub_map))) {\n  h <- hub_map$human[i]\n  r <- hub_map$rat[i]\n\n  if (r %in% rownames(exp_mat)) {\n    hub_map$in_exp[i] <- r\n  } else if (h %in% rownames(exp_mat)) {\n    hub_map$in_exp[i] <- h\n  } else {\n    # 模糊匹配 (忽略大小写)\n    idx <- grep(paste0(\"^\", r, \"$\"), rownames(exp_mat), ignore.case = TRUE)\n    if (length(idx) > 0) hub_map$in_exp[i] <- rownames(exp_mat)[idx[1]]\n  }\n}\n\nhub_found <- hub_map %>% dplyr::filter(!is.na(in_exp))\ncat(sprintf(\"  Hub 基因在表达矩阵中匹配: %d / %d\\n\", nrow(hub_found), nrow(hub_map)))\n\nif (nrow(hub_found) > 0) {\n  cat(\"  匹配到:\", paste(hub_found$in_exp, collapse = \", \"), \"\\n\")\n}\n```\n\n## 8.3 Hub 基因热图\n\n```{r hub_heatmap, fig.width=10, fig.height=8}\nif (nrow(hub_found) == 0) {\n  cat(\"  ⚠ 未在表达矩阵中找到任何 Hub 基因。\\n\")\n  cat(\"    可能原因: 基因符号格式差异或物种映射问题\\n\")\n} else {\n\n  # 提取 Hub 基因表达\n  hub_exp <- exp_mat[hub_found$in_exp, , drop = FALSE]\n\n  # 确保样本顺序一致\n  common_samples <- intersect(colnames(hub_exp), rownames(pd))\n  hub_exp <- hub_exp[, common_samples, drop = FALSE]\n  pd_sub  <- pd[common_samples, , drop = FALSE]\n\n  # ── 热图 ──\n  anno_col <- data.frame(\n    Group = pd_sub$group,\n    row.names = common_samples\n  )\n\n  group_colors <- c(\n    \"Young_sham\" = \"#3498DB\", \"Aged_sham\" = \"#27AE60\",\n    \"Young_MCAO\" = \"#F39C12\", \"Aged_MCAO\" = \"#E74C3C\"\n  )\n  ann_colors <- list(Group = (nrow(hub_found) > 0) {\n  stat_results <- lapply(seq_len(nrow(hub_found)), function(i) {\n    gene_r <- hub_found$in_exp[i]\n    gene_h <- hub_found$human[i]\n\n    vals_mcao <- as.numeric(hub_exp[gene_r, pd_sub$group == \"Aged_MCAO\"])\n    vals_sham <- as.numeric(hub_exp[gene_r, pd_sub$group == \"Aged_sham\"])\n\n    if (length(vals_mcao) >= 2 && length(vals_sham) >= 2) {\n      tt <- tryCatch(t.test(vals_mcao, vals_sham), error = function(e) NULL)\n      wt <- tryCatch(wilcox.test(vals_mcao, vals_sham), error = function(e) NULL)\n\n      data.frame(\n        gene_human  = gene_h,\n        gene_rat    = gene_r,\n        mean_MCAO   = mean(vals_mcao),\n        mean_sham   = mean(vals_sham),\n        logFC       = log2(mean(vals_mcao) / mean(vals_sham)),\n        t_pvalue    = if (!is.null(tt)) tt$p.value else NA,\n        wilcox_pvalue = if (!is.null(wt)) wt$p.value else NA,\n        stringsAsFactors = FALSE\n      )\n    } else {\n      NULL\n    }\n  })\n\n Copilot 2026/04/19 19:22

原因很清楚：**Venn 图中心显示的是严格的三者交集 (intersection_3way)，但 04_intersection_genes.csv 保存的是 target_genes，当三者交集 < 5 个时会自动扩大为 DEG ∩ (疾病 ∪ 中药)**。

具体逻辑（第 455–467 行）：
- **三者交集 ≥ 5** → target_genes = intersection_3way，两者一致
- **三者交集 1–4 个** → target_genes 扩大为 DEG ∩ (疾病 ∪ 中药)，比 Venn 中心数字大
- **三者交集 = 0** → target_genes = DEG ∩ (疾病 ∪ 中药)

所以当三者交集较少触发了 fallback 策略时，CSV 里的基因数会多于 Venn 图中心标注的数字。

**您希望怎么处理？** 常见方案：
1. **CSV 只保存严格三者交集** — Venn 和 CSV 一致
2. **Venn 图上额外标注 fallback 的总数** — 保留当前策略但加说明
3. **保持原样** — 这是设计上的 fallback 机制

这恰好说明了之前 fallback 机制的影响——如果之前 Venn 中心显示的也是 3 个但 CSV 里更多，那就是旧代码 fallback 扩大了（DEG ∩ (Disease ∪ Herb)）。现在修改后严格用三者交集，Venn 和 CSV 会一致显示 3 个。

run_in_terminal 
{
  "command": "cd /Users/yuzuan/Desktop/fastGEO/test/0420 && Rscript -e '\nsuppressWarnings(suppressMessages({\nlibrary(readxl); library(pheatmap)\n\ndf <- read_xlsx(\"core_table1.xlsx\")\nexpr_cols <- c(\"No_1\",\"No_2\",\"No_3\",\"Hy_1\",\"Hy_2\",\"Hy_3\")\nmat <- as.matrix(df[, expr_cols]); rownames(mat) <- df$gene\nlog_mat <- log2(mat + 1)\n\nset1 <- c(\"PCNA\",\"MKI67\",\"CCND1\",\"CDK1\",\"E2F1\",\"TOP2A\",\"PLK1\",\"BIRC5\",\"FOXM1\",\"MCM2\",\n          \"GDNF\",\"CXCL12\",\"CSF1\",\"ETV5\",\"ZBTB16\")\nset2 <- c(\"EP300\",\"KAT2A\",\"OXCT1\",\"SIRT5\",\"SIRT7\",\"HDAC2\",\"MLLT1\",\"MLLT3\")\n\n# 提取这些基因的表达，计算相关性 (样本间)\nall_genes <- c(set1, set2)\nsub_mat <- t(log_mat[all_genes, ])  # 转置: 行=样本, 列=基因\ncor_mat <- cor(sub_mat, method = \"pearson\")\n\n# 只取 set1(行) x set2(列) 的交叉相关性\ncross_cor <- cor_mat[set1, set2]\n\npheatmap(cross_cor,\n         display_numbers = TRUE, number_format = \"%.2f\",\n         color = colorRampPalette(c(\"#4575b4\",\"white\",\"#d73027\"))(100),\n         cluster_rows = TRUE, cluster_cols = TRUE,\n         main = \"Gene-Gene Correlation (Set1 vs Set2)\",\n         fontsize = 9, fontsize_number = 7,\n         filename = \"09_gene_correlation_heatmap.pdf\", width = 9, height = 8)\ncat(\"相关性热图已保存\\n\")\n\n# 也做一个全部 23 基因的完整相关性矩阵\nanno_row <- data.frame(\n  Set = c(rep(\"Proliferation/Signaling\", length(set1)), rep(\"Epigenetic/Metabolic\", length(set2))),\n  row.names = all_genes\n)\n\npheatmap(cor_mat,\n         display_numbers = TRUE, number_format = \"%.2f\",\n         annotation_row = anno_row, annotation_col = anno_row,\n         color = colorRampPalette(c(\"#4575b4\",\"white\",\"#d73027\"))(100),\n         main = \"Gene-Gene Correlation (All 23 Genes)\",\n         fontsize = 8, fontsize_number = 5,\n         filename = \"09b_gene_correlation_full.pdf\", width = 12, height = 11)\ncat(\"完整相关性热图已保存\\n\")\n}))\n' 2>&1",

参考了配色方案。用 ComplexHeatmap + ggsci 重做 Top20 热图：

▸ Tool calls (1)
run_in_terminal 
{
  "command": "cd /Users/yuzuan/Desktop/fastGEO/test/0420 && Rscript -e '\nsuppressWarnings(suppressMessages({\nlibrary(readxl); library(ComplexHeatmap); library(ggsci); library(circlize); library(grid)\n\ndf <- read_xlsx(\"core_table1.xlsx\")\nexpr_cols <- c(\"No_1\",\"No_2\",\"No_3\",\"Hy_1\",\"Hy_2\",\"Hy_3\")\nmat <- as.matrix(df[, expr_cols]); rownames(mat) <- df$gene\nlog_mat <- log2(mat + 1)\n\ndeg <- df[df$pvalue < 0.05 & abs(df$logFC) > 0.585, ]\ndeg$regulation <- ifelse(deg$logFC > 0, \"Up\", \"Down\")\n\ntop_up   <- head(deg[order(-deg$logFC), ], 10)\ntop_down <- head(deg[order(deg$logFC), ], 10)\ntop20 <- rbind(top_up, top_down)\n\n# 标准化\nsub_exp <- log_mat[top20$gene, ]\nsub_scaled <- t(scale(t(sub_exp)))\n\n# ggsci 配色\nnpg_colors <- pal_npg(\"nrc\")(10)\nlancet_colors <- pal_lancet(\"lanonc\")(9)\ngroup_colors <- c(\"No\" = npg_colors[4], \"Hy\" = npg_colors[1])\nregulation_colors <- c(\"Up\" = lancet_colors[1], \"Down\" = lancet_colors[2])\nheatmap_colors <- colorRampPalette(c(npg_colors[3], \"white\", npg_colors[1]))(100)\n\n# 注释\ngroup_vec <- c(rep(\"No\", 3), rep(\"Hy\", 3))\nnames(group_vec) <- colnames(sub_scaled)\nreg_vec <- top20$regulation; names(reg_vec) <- top20$gene\n\nha_top <- HeatmapAnnotation(\n  Group = group_vec,\n  col = list(Group = group_colors),\n  show_annotation_name = FALSE,\n  annotation_legend_param = list(Group = list(title = NULL))\n)\n\nra_left <- rowAnnotation(\n  Regulation = reg_vec,\n  col = list(Regulation = regulation_colors),\n  show_annotation_name = FALSE,\n  annotation_legend_param = list(Regulation = list(title = NULL)),\n  width = unit(0.5, \"cm\")\n)\n\np <- Heatmap(sub_scaled,\n  col = heatmap_colors, name = \"Z-score\",\n  heatmap_legend_param = list(direction = \"horizontal\",\n    title_position = \"topcenter\", legend_width = unit(6, \"cm\")),\n  show_row_names = TRUE, show_column_names = FALSE,\n  show_row_dend = FALSE, show_column_dend = FALSE,\n  top_annotation = ha_top, left_annotation = ra_left,\n  column_split = group_vec, row_split = reg_vec,\n  row_names_gp = gpar(fontsize = 10),\n  column_title_gp = gpar(fontsize = 12, fontface = \"bold\"),\n  row_title_gp = gpar(fontsize = 12, fontface = \"bold\"),\n  cluster_rows = TRUE, cluster_columns = TRUE, border = TRUE\n)\n\npdf(\"10_top20_DEG_heatmap.pdf\", width = 8, height = 7)\ndraw(p, heatmap_legend_side = \"bottom\", annotation_legend_side = \"bottom\", merge_legend = TRUE)\ndev.off()\ncat(\"Top20 DEG 热图已用 ComplexHeatmap+ggsci 重做\\n\")\n}))\n' 2>&1",
  "explanation": "用 ComplexHeatmap + ggsci 配色重做 Top20 热图",

run_in_terminal 
{
  "command": "cd /Users/yuzuan/Desktop/fastGEO/test/0420 && Rscript -e '\nsuppressWarnings(suppressMessages({\nlibrary(readxl); library(ggplot2); library(ggrepel)\n\ndf <- read_xlsx(\"core_table1.xlsx\")\nexpr_cols <- c(\"No_1\",\"No_2\",\"No_3\",\"Hy_1\",\"Hy_2\",\"Hy_3\")\nmat <- as.matrix(df[, expr_cols]); rownames(mat) <- df$gene\nlog_mat <- log2(mat + 1)\n\n# 过滤零方差基因 (参考 fastGEO: expM[apply(expM,1,sd)!=0,])\nlog_mat_f <- log_mat[apply(log_mat, 1, sd) != 0, ]\n\npca <- prcomp(t(log_mat_f), scale = TRUE)\nvar_explained <- pca$sdev^2 / sum(pca$sdev^2)\nvar_pct <- round(var_explained * 100, 2)\n\ngroup <- c(rep(\"No\", 3), rep(\"Hy\", 3))\npca_df <- data.frame(\n  PC1 = pca$x[, 1], PC2 = pca$x[, 2],\n  group = group, Sample = colnames(log_mat_f)\n)\n\n# fastGEO 默认配色\nmy_cols <- c(\"#1C79B7\", \"#F38329\")\n\np <- ggplot(pca_df, aes(x = PC1, y = PC2, color = group)) +\n  geom_point(size = 3) +\n  geom_text_repel(aes(label = Sample), size = 3.5,\n                  point.padding = unit(0.5, \"lines\"),\n                  show.legend = FALSE, max.overlaps = Inf) +\n  geom_hline(yintercept = 0, lty = 4, col = \"black\", lwd = 0.6) +\n  geom_vline(xintercept = 0, lty = 4, col = \"black\", lwd = 0.6) +\n  stat_ellipse(aes(x = PC1, y = PC2), linetype = 2, size = 0.5,\n               level = 0.95, show.legend = FALSE) +\n  scale_color_manual(values = my_cols) +\n  labs(x = paste0(\"PC1(\", var_pct[1], \"%)\"),\n       y = paste0(\"PC2(\", var_pct[2], \"%)\"),\n       title = \"PCA\", color = \"\") +\n  theme_bw(base_size = 14) +\n  theme(\n    panel.grid.major = element_blank(),\n    panel.grid.minor = element_blank(),\n    plot.title = element_text(hjust = 0.5, face = \"bold\"),\n    legend.position = \"top\"\n  ) +\n  guides(color = guide_legend(override.aes = list(size = 3)))\n\nggsave(\"02_PCA.pdf\", p, width = 5, height = 5)\ncat(\"PCA 图已按 fastGEO 风格更新\\n\")\n}))\n' 2>&1",
